[30;1m501 | [0m[35m- *Backwards-incompatible*: Refactor automatic documentation generation. At[0m
[30;1m502 | [0m[35m  import time, each decorator stores information under its own namespace in[0m
[30;1m503 | [0m[35m  the view function's ``_apidoc`` attribute. Then at app init time, the[0m
